<p><strong>ENHANCE EXPERIENCE, INC.</strong><br>
<strong>PRIVACY POLICY</strong></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Last Updated June 3, 2022</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Welcome to the websites (collectively, the â</span><b>Site</b><span style="font-weight: 400;">â) of Enhance Experience, Inc. (â</span><b>Enhance</b><span style="font-weight: 400;">,â â</span><b>we</b><span style="font-weight: 400;">,â â</span><b>us</b><span style="font-weight: 400;">,â or â</span><b>our</b><span style="font-weight: 400;">â). Through the Site, we provide sales and marketing information about our company, our video games, our interactive art, and our synesthesia engine (such information, together with the Site, the â</span><b>Service</b><span style="font-weight: 400;">â).&nbsp;</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This Privacy Policy explains what Personal Data (defined below) we collect, how we use and share that data, and your choices concerning our data practices. This Privacy Policy is incorporated into and forms part of our End User License Agreement.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Before using the Service or submitting any Personal Data to Enhance, please review this Privacy Policy carefully and </span><a href="#contact_us"><span style="font-weight: 400;">contact us</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> if you have any questions. By using the Service, you agree to the practices described in this Privacy Policy. If you do not agree to this Privacy Policy, please do not access the Site or otherwise use the Service.</span><b></b></p>
<p><b>1. PERSONAL DATA WE COLLECT</b></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">We collect information that alone or in combination with other information in our possession could be used to identify you (â</span><b>Personal Data</b><span style="font-weight: 400;">â) as follows:</span></p>
<p><b>Personal Data You Provide:</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> We collect Personal Data from you when you sign up for our mailing list, request a demo, apply for a job, download an application for your console, ask for help when using our Service, or contact us. The Personal Data we collect varies depending on what you choose to share, but it may include your name, email, resume, and other information you provide in connection with your job application such as references and work history.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">We also have pages on social media sites like Instagram, Facebook, Twitter, Discord, and YouTube (â</span><b>Social Media Pages</b><span style="font-weight: 400;">â). When you interact with our Social Media Pages, we will collect Personal Data that you elect to provide to us, such as your contact details. In addition, the companies that host our Social Media Pages may provide us with aggregate information and analytics regarding the use of our Social Media Pages. In addition, if you review one of our games through one of our platform partners (such as Microsoft, PlayStation, Oculus, Steam or Epic Games), we may collect any Personal Information provided by you and associated with your review (such as your name, the contents of your review, and the data/time of your review).</span></p>
<p><b>Internet Activity Data:</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> When you visit, use, and interact with the Service, we may receive certain information about your visit, use, or interactions. For example, we may monitor the number of people that visit the Service, peak hours of visits, which page(s) are visited, the domains our visitors come from (e.g., google.com, yahoo.com, etc.), and which browsers people use to access the Service (e.g., Chrome, Firefox, Microsoft Internet Explorer, etc.), broad geographical information, and navigation pattern. In particular, the following information is created and automatically logged in our systems:&nbsp;</span></p>
<ul>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><b>Log Data</b><span style="font-weight: 400;">: Information that your browser automatically sends whenever you visit the Site. Log Data includes your Internet Protocol address, browser type and settings, the date and time of your request, and how you interacted with the Site.&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><b>Cookies Data:</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> Please see the â</span><a href="#cookies"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Cookies</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">â section below to learn more about how we use cookies.</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><b>Device Data</b><span style="font-weight: 400;">: Includes name of the device, operating system, and browser you are using. Information collected may depend on the type of device you use and its settings.&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><b>Usage Data</b><span style="font-weight: 400;">: We collect information about how you use our Service, such as the types of content that you view or engage with, the features you use, the actions you take, and the time, frequency, and duration of your activities.</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><b>Location Data</b><span style="font-weight: 400;">: We derive a rough estimate of your location from your IP address.&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><b>Email Open/Click Data: </b><span style="font-weight: 400;">We use pixels in our email campaigns that allow us to collect your email and IP address as well as the date and time you open an email or click on any links in the email.</span></li>
</ul>
<p><a id="cookies"></a><b>Cookies:</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> We use cookies to operate and administer our Site, gather usage data on our Site, and improve your experience on it. A âcookieâ is a piece of information sent to your browser by a website you visit. Cookies can be stored on your computer for different periods of time. Some cookies expire after a certain amount of time, or upon logging out (session cookies), others survive after your browser is closed until a defined expiration date set in the cookie (as determined by the third party placing it), and help recognize your computer when you open your browser and browse the Internet again (persistent cookies). For more details on cookies please visit </span><a href="http://www.allaboutcookies.org/" rel="noopener noreferrer" onclick="javascript:window.open('http://www.allaboutcookies.org/'); return false;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">All About Cookies</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">On most web browsers, you will find a âhelpâ section on the toolbar. Please refer to this section for information on how to receive a notification when you are receiving a new cookie and how to turn cookies off. Please see the links below for guidance on how to modify your web browserâs settings on the most popular browsers:</span></p>
<ul>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><a href="http://windows.microsoft.com/en-gb/internet-explorer/delete-manage-cookies#ie=ie-11" rel="noopener noreferrer" onclick="javascript:window.open('http://windows.microsoft.com/en-gb/internet-explorer/delete-manage-cookies#ie=ie-11'); return false;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Internet Explorer</span></a></li>

<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><a href="https://support.google.com/accounts/answer/61416?hl=en" rel="noopener noreferrer" onclick="javascript:window.open('https://support.google.com/accounts/answer/61416?hl=en'); return false;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Google Chrome</span></a></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><a href="https://support.apple.com/guide/safari/manage-cookies-and-website-data-sfri11471/mac" rel="noopener noreferrer" onclick="javascript:window.open('https://support.apple.com/guide/safari/manage-cookies-and-website-data-sfri11471/mac'); return false;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Apple Safari</span></a></li>

<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Please note that if you limit the ability of websites to set cookies, you may be unable to access certain parts of the Site and you may not be able to benefit from the full functionality of the Site.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Advertising networks may use cookies to collect Personal Data. Most advertising networks offer you a way to opt out of targeted advertising. If you would like to find out more information, please visit the Network Advertising Initiativeâs online resources at </span><a href="http://www.networkadvertising.org" rel="noopener noreferrer" onclick="javascript:window.open('http://www.networkadvertising.org/'); return false;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">http://www.networkadvertising.org</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> and follow the opt-out instructions there.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">If you access the Site on your mobile device, you may not be able to control tracking technologies through the settings.&nbsp;</span></p>
<p><b>Analytics:</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> We use </span><span style="font-weight: 400;">Google Analytics, a web analytics service provided by Google, Inc. (âGoogleâ). <p><b>Online Tracking and Do Not Track Signals</b><span style="font-weight: 400;">: We and our third party service providers, including Facebook, may use cookies, pixels, or other tracking technologies to collect information about your browsing activities over time and across different websites following your use of the Site and use that information to send targeted advertisements. <p><b>2. HOW WE USE PERSONAL DATA</b></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">We may use Personal Data for the following purposes:</span></p>
<ul>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">To provide the Service and send you any information you request about our games or software;</span></li>

<p><b>Aggregated Information.</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> We may aggregate Personal Data and use the aggregated information to analyze the effectiveness of our Service, to improve and add features to our Service, and for other similar purposes. We may collect aggregated information through the Service, through cookies, and through other means described in this Privacy Policy.</span></p>
<p><b>Marketing. </b><span style="font-weight: 400;">We may use your Personal Data to contact you to tell you about products or services we believe may be of interest to you. <p><b>3. SHARING AND DISCLOSURE OF PERSONAL DATA</b></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">In certain circumstances we may share the categories of Personal Data described above without further notice to you, unless required by the law, with the following categories of third parties:</span></p>
<ul>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><b>Vendors and Service Providers: </b><span style="font-weight: 400;">To assist us in meeting business operations needs and to perform certain services and functions, we may share Personal Data with vendors and service providers, including providers of hosting services, cloud services, and other information technology services providers, email communication software and email newsletter services, advertising and marketing services, payment processors, customer relationship management and customer support services, and analytics services. Pursuant to our instructions, these parties will access, process, or store Personal Data in the course of performing their duties to us.&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><b>Business Transfers:</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> If we are involved in a merger, acquisition, financing due diligence, reorganization, bankruptcy, receivership, sale of all or a portion of our assets, or transition of service to another provider (collectively a âTransactionâ), your Personal Data and other information may be shared in the diligence process with counterparties and others assisting with the Transaction and transferred to a successor or affiliate as part of that Transaction along with other assets.</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><b>Legal Requirements:</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> If required to do so by law or in the good faith belief that such action is necessary to (i) comply with a legal obligation, including to meet national security or law enforcement requirements, (ii) protect and defend our rights or property, (iii) prevent fraud, (iv) act in urgent circumstances to protect the personal safety of users of the Service, or the public, or (v) protect against legal liability.</span></li>

<p><b>4. UPDATE YOUR INFORMATION</b></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Please </span><a href="#contact_us"><span style="font-weight: 400;">contact us</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> if you need to delete, change or correct your Personal Data.&nbsp;</span></p>
<p><b>5. CHILDREN</b></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Our Service is not directed to children who are under the age of 16. Enhance does not knowingly collect Personal Data from children under the age of 16. If you have reason to believe that a child under the age of 16 has provided Personal Data to Enhance through the Service please </span><a href="#contact_us"><span style="font-weight: 400;">contact us</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> and we will endeavor to delete that information from our databases.</span></p>
<p><b>6. LINKS TO OTHER WEBSITES</b></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The Service may contain links to other websites not operated or controlled by Enhance, including social media services (â</span><b>Third Party Sites</b><span style="font-weight: 400;">â). The information that you share with Third Party Sites will be governed by the specific privacy policies and terms of service of the Third Party Sites and not by this Privacy Policy. By providing these links we do not imply that we endorse or have reviewed these sites. Please contact the Third Party Sites directly for information on their privacy practices and policies.&nbsp;</span></p>
<p><b>7. SECURITY</b></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">You use the Service at your own risk. We implement commercially reasonable technical, administrative, and organizational measures to protect Personal Data both online and offline from loss, misuse, and unauthorized access, disclosure, alteration, or destruction. However, no Internet or e-mail transmission is ever fully secure or error free. In particular, e-mail sent to or from us may not be secure. Therefore, you should take special care in deciding what information you send to us via the Service or e-mail. Please keep this in mind when disclosing any Personal Data to Enhance via the Internet. In addition, we are not responsible for circumvention of any privacy settings or security measures contained on the Service, or third party websites.</span></p>
<p><b>8. INTERNATIONAL USERS</b></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">By using our Service, you understand and acknowledge that your Personal Data will be transferred from your location to our facilities and servers in the United States.</span></p>
<p><b>9. YOUR CHOICES</b></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">In certain circumstances providing Personal Data is optional. However, if you choose not to provide Personal Data that is needed to use some features of our Service, you may be unable to use those features. You can also </span><a href="#contact_us"><span style="font-weight: 400;">contact us</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> to ask us to delete, update or correct your Personal Data.</span></p>
<p><b>10. CHANGES TO THE PRIVACY POLICY</b></p>

WITHOUT LIMITATION TO THE FOREGOING, ENHANCE PROVIDES NO WARRANTY OR UNDERTAKING, AND MAKES NO REPRESENTATION OF ANY KIND THAT THE GAME WILL MEET YOUR REQUIREMENTS, ACHIEVE ANY INTENDED RESULTS, BE COMPATIBLE, OR WORK WITH ANY OTHER SOFTWARE, GAMES, SYSTEMS, OR SERVICES, OPERATE WITHOUT INTERRUPTION, MEET ANY PERFORMANCE OR RELIABILITY STANDARDS OR BE ERROR-FREE, OR THAT ANY ERRORS OR DEFECTS CAN OR WILL BE CORRECTED.</span></p>

<p><b>7. <span style="text-decoration: underline;">Limitation of Liability</span></b></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">TO THE FULLEST EXTENT PERMITTED BY APPLICABLE LAW, IN NO EVENT WILL ENHANCE OR ITS AFFILIATES, OR ANY OF ITS OR THEIR RESPECTIVE LICENSORS OR SERVICE PROVIDERS, HAVE ANY LIABILITY ARISING FROM OR RELATED TO YOUR USE OF OR INABILITY TO USE THE GAME OR THE CONTENT AND SERVICES FOR: (A) ANY PERSONAL INJURY, PROPERTY DAMAGE, LOST PROFITS, COST OF SUBSTITUTE GOODS OR SERVICES, LOSS OF DATA, LOSS OF GOODWILL, BUSINESS INTERRUPTION, COMPUTER FAILURE OR MALFUNCTION, OR ANY OTHER CONSEQUENTIAL, INCIDENTAL, INDIRECT, EXEMPLARY, SPECIAL, OR PUNITIVE DAMAGES; OR (B) ANY DIRECT DAMAGES IN AMOUNTS THAT IN THE AGGREGATE EXCEED THE AMOUNT ACTUALLY PAID BY YOU FOR THE GAME.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">THE FOREGOING LIMITATIONS WILL APPLY WHETHER SUCH DAMAGES ARISE OUT OF BREACH OF CONTRACT, TORT (INCLUDING NEGLIGENCE), OR OTHERWISE AND REGARDLESS OF WHETHER SUCH DAMAGES WERE FORESEEABLE OR ENHANCE WAS ADVISED OF THE POSSIBILITY OF SUCH DAMAGES. SOME JURISDICTIONS DO NOT ALLOW CERTAIN LIMITATIONS OF LIABILITY SO SOME OR ALL OF THE ABOVE LIMITATIONS OF LIABILITY MAY NOT APPLY TO YOU.</span></p>
<p><b>8. <span style="text-decoration: underline;">Dispute Resolution By Binding Arbitration: PLEASE READ THIS SECTION CAREFULLY AS IT AFFECTS YOUR RIGHTS&nbsp;</span></b></p>
<ul>
<li><span style="font-weight: 400;">8.1 <span style="text-decoration: underline;">Agreement to Arbitrate</span></span><span style="font-weight: 400;">.&nbsp; This Dispute Resolution by Binding Arbitration section is referred to in this Agreement as the âArbitration Agreement.â&nbsp; You agree that any and all disputes or claims that have arisen or may arise between you and Enhance, whether arising out of or relating to this Agreement (including any alleged breach thereof), the Services, any advertising, any aspect of the relationship or transactions between us, shall be resolved exclusively through final and binding arbitration, rather than a court, in accordance with the terms of this Arbitration Agreement, except that you may assert individual claims in small claims court, if your claims qualify.&nbsp; Further, this Arbitration Agreement does not preclude you from bringing issues to the attention of federal, state, or local agencies, and such agencies can, if the law allows, seek relief against us on your behalf.&nbsp; You agree that, by entering into this Agreement, you and Enhance are each waiving the right to a trial by jury or to participate in a class action.&nbsp; Your rights will be determined by a neutral arbitrator, not a judge or jury.&nbsp; The Federal Arbitration Act governs the interpretation and enforcement of this Arbitration Agreement.</span></li>
<li>8.2 <span style="text-decoration: underline;">Prohibition of Class and Representative Actions and Non-Individualized Relief</span>.<br>
<b><i>YOU AND ENHANCE AGREE THAT EACH OF US MAY BRING CLAIMS AGAINST THE OTHER ONLY ON AN INDIVIDUAL BASIS AND NOT AS A PLAINTIFF OR CLASS MEMBER IN ANY PURPORTED CLASS OR REPRESENTATIVE ACTION OR PROCEEDING.&nbsp; UNLESS BOTH YOU AND ENHANCE AGREE OTHERWISE, THE ARBITRATOR MAY NOT CONSOLIDATE OR JOIN MORE THAN ONE PERSONâS OR PARTYâS CLAIMS AND MAY NOT OTHERWISE PRESIDE OVER ANY FORM OF A CONSOLIDATED, REPRESENTATIVE, OR CLASS PROCEEDING.&nbsp; ALSO, THE ARBITRATOR MAY AWARD RELIEF (INCLUDING MONETARY, INJUNCTIVE, AND DECLARATORY RELIEF) ONLY IN FAVOR OF THE INDIVIDUAL PARTY SEEKING RELIEF AND ONLY TO THE EXTENT NECESSARY TO PROVIDE RELIEF NECESSITATED BY THAT PARTYâS INDIVIDUAL CLAIM(S), EXCEPT THAT YOU MAY PURSUE A CLAIM FOR AND THE ARBITRATOR MAY AWARD PUBLIC INJUNCTIVE RELIEF UNDER APPLICABLE LAW TO THE EXTENT REQUIRED FOR THE ENFORCEABILITY OF THIS PROVISION.&nbsp; </i></b></li>
<li>8.3 <span style="text-decoration: underline;">Pre-Arbitration Dispute Resolution</span>.&nbsp; Enhance is always interested in resolving disputes amicably and efficiently, and most customer concerns can be resolved quickly and to the customerâs satisfaction by emailing customer support at hello@enhance-experience.com.&nbsp; If such efforts prove unsuccessful, a party who intends to seek arbitration must first send to the other, by certified mail, a written Notice of Dispute (âNoticeâ).&nbsp; The Notice to Enhance should be sent to 100 Moffett Blvd, Suite B301, Mountain View, CA 94043 USA (âNotice Addressâ).&nbsp; The Notice must (i) describe the nature and basis of the claim or dispute and (ii) set forth the specific relief sought.&nbsp; If Enhance and you do not resolve the claim within sixty (60) calendar days after the Notice is received, you or Enhance may commence an arbitration proceeding.&nbsp; During the arbitration, the amount of any settlement offer made by Enhance or you shall not be disclosed to the arbitrator until after the arbitrator determines the amount, if any, to which you or Enhance is entitled.</li>
<li>8.4 <span style="text-decoration: underline;">Arbitration Procedures</span>.&nbsp; Arbitration will be conducted by a neutral arbitrator in accordance with the American Arbitration Associationâs (âAAAâ) rules and procedures, including the AAAâs Consumer Arbitration Rules (collectively, the âAAA Rulesâ), as modified by this Arbitration Agreement.&nbsp; For information on the AAA, please visit its website, <a href="http://www.adr.org" rel="noopener noreferrer" onclick="javascript:window.open('http://www.adr.org/'); return false;">http://www.adr.org</a>.&nbsp; Information about the AAA Rules and fees for consumer disputes can be found at the AAAâs consumer arbitration page, <a href="http://www.adr.org/" rel="noopener noreferrer" onclick="javascript:window.open('http://www.adr.org/'); return false;">http://www.adr.org/</a> as may be updated from time to time.&nbsp; If there is any inconsistency between any term of the AAA Rules and any term of this Arbitration Agreement, the applicable terms of this Arbitration Agreement will control unless the arbitrator determines that the application of the inconsistent Arbitration Agreement terms would not result in a fundamentally fair arbitration.&nbsp; The arbitrator must also follow the provisions of this Agreement as a court would.&nbsp; All issues are for the arbitrator to decide, including, but not limited to, issues relating to the scope, enforceability, and arbitrability of this Arbitration Agreement.&nbsp; Although arbitration proceedings are usually simpler and more streamlined than trials and other judicial proceedings, the arbitrator can award the same damages and relief on an individual basis that a court can award to an individual under this Agreement and applicable law.&nbsp; Decisions by the arbitrator are enforceable in court and may be overturned by a court only for very limited reasons.Unless Enhance and you agree otherwise, any arbitration hearings will take place in a reasonably convenient location for both parties with due consideration of their ability to travel and other pertinent circumstances.&nbsp; If the parties are unable to agree on a location, the determination shall be made by AAA.&nbsp; If your claim is for $10,000 or less, Enhance agrees that you may choose whether the arbitration will be conducted solely on the basis of documents submitted to the arbitrator, through a telephonic hearing, or by an in-person hearing as established by the AAA Rules.&nbsp; If your claim exceeds $10,000, the right to a hearing will be determined by the AAA Rules.&nbsp; Regardless of the manner in which the arbitration is conducted, the arbitrator shall issue a reasoned written decision sufficient to explain the essential findings and conclusions on which the award is based.</li>
<li>8.5 <span style="text-decoration: underline;">Costs of Arbitration</span>.&nbsp; Payment of all filing, administration, and arbitrator fees (collectively, the âArbitration Feesâ) will be governed by the AAA Rules, unless otherwise provided in this Arbitration Agreement.&nbsp; If the value of the relief sought is $75,000 or less, at your request, Enhance will pay all Arbitration Fees.&nbsp; If the value of relief sought is more than $75,000 and you are able to demonstrate to the arbitrator that you are economically unable to pay your portion of the Arbitration Fees or if the arbitrator otherwise determines for any reason that you should not be required to pay your portion of the Arbitration Fees, Enhance will pay your portion of such fees.&nbsp; In addition, if you demonstrate to the arbitrator that the costs of arbitration will be prohibitive as compared to the costs of litigation, Enhance will pay as much of the Arbitration Fees as the arbitrator deems necessary to prevent the arbitration from being cost-prohibitive.&nbsp; Any payment of attorneysâ fees will be governed by the AAA Rules.</li>
<li>8.6 <span style="text-decoration: underline;">Confidentiality</span>.&nbsp; All aspects of the arbitration proceeding, and any ruling, decision, or award by the arbitrator, will be strictly confidential for the benefit of all parties.</li>
<li>8.7 <span style="text-decoration: underline;">Severability</span>.&nbsp; If a court or the arbitrator decides that any term or provision of this Arbitration Agreement (other than the subsection (b) titled âProhibition of Class and Representative Actions and Non-Individualized Reliefâ above) is invalid or unenforceable, the parties agree to replace such term or provision with a term or provision that is valid and enforceable and that comes closest to expressing the intention of the invalid or unenforceable term or provision, and this Arbitration Agreement shall be enforceable as so modified.&nbsp; If a court or the arbitrator decides that any of the provisions of subsection (b) above titled âProhibition of Class and Representative Actions and Non-Individualized Reliefâ are invalid or unenforceable, then the entirety of this Arbitration Agreement shall be null and void, unless such provisions are deemed to be invalid or unenforceable solely with respect to claims for public injunctive relief.&nbsp; The remainder of the Agreement will continue to apply.</li>
<li>8.8 <span style="text-decoration: underline;">Future Changes to Arbitration Agreement</span>.&nbsp; Notwithstanding any provision in this Agreement to the contrary, Enhance agrees that if it makes any future change to this Arbitration Agreement (other than a change to the Notice Address) while you are a user of the Services, you may reject any such change by sending Enhance written notice within thirty (30) calendar days of the change to the Notice Address provided above.&nbsp; By rejecting any future change, you are agreeing that you will arbitrate any dispute between us in accordance with the language of this Arbitration Agreement as of the date you first accepted this Agreement (or accepted any subsequent changes to this Agreement).</li>
</ul>
<p><b>9. <span style="text-decoration: underline;">Miscellaneous</span></b></p>
<ul>
<li style="list-style-type: none;">

<li><span style="font-weight: 400;">9.1 <span style="text-decoration: underline;">Export Regulation</span></span><span style="font-weight: 400;">. The Game may be subject to export control laws. You shall not, directly or indirectly, export, re-export, or release the Game to, or make the Game accessible from, any jurisdiction or country to which export, re-export, or release is prohibited by law, rule, or regulation. You shall comply with all applicable laws, regulations, and rules, and complete all required undertakings (including obtaining any necessary export license or other governmental approval), prior to exporting, re-exporting, releasing, or otherwise making the Game available outside your jurisdiction or country.</span></li>
<li>9.2 <span style="text-decoration: underline;">Severability</span>. If any provision of this Agreement is illegal or unenforceable under applicable law, the remainder of the provision will be amended to achieve as closely as possible the effect of the original term and all other provisions of this Agreement will continue in full force and effect.</li>
<li>9.3 <span style="text-decoration: underline;">Governing Law</span>. This Agreement is governed by and construed in accordance with the internal laws of Japan without giving effect to any choice or conflict of law provision or rule. Any legal suit, action, or proceeding arising out of or related to this Agreement or the Game shall be instituted exclusively in the Tokyo District Court for the first instance. You waive any and all objections to the exercise of jurisdiction over you by such courts and to venue in such courts.</li>
<li>9.4 <span style="text-decoration: underline;">Waiver</span>.&nbsp; No failure to exercise, and no delay in exercising, on the part of either party, any right or any power hereunder shall operate as a waiver thereof, nor shall any single or partial exercise of any right or power hereunder preclude further exercise of that or any other right hereunder. In the event of a conflict between this Agreement and any applicable purchase or other terms, the terms of this Agreement shall govern.</li>
<li><span style="font-weight: 400;">9.5 <span style="text-decoration: underline;">Entire Agreement</span></span><span style="font-weight: 400;">. This Agreement, our Privacy Policy, our Community Guidelines and any other terms that reference this Agreement constitute the entire agreement between you and Enhance with respect to the Game and supersede all prior or contemporaneous understandings and agreements, whether written or oral, with respect to the Game.</span></li>

<p><strong>ENHANCE EXPERIENCE INC.<br>
</strong><strong>COMMUNITY GUIDELINES</strong><strong>&nbsp;</strong></p>
<p><strong>Date of Last Revision: June 11, 2021 </strong></p>
<p>At Enhance, our mission is to provide an exciting, community oriented, multiplayer, multi-sensory platform experience where users can interact safely. To achieve this goal, we ask that all users participate in such a way that promotes a friendly, positive-experience community.&nbsp; In addition to any other applicable End User License Agreement or Terms of Service that applies to your use of our website, games or platform (collectively, the âServiceâ), we have prepared the following guidelines for our community. These apply to all users, user generated content and user activity on our website (located at https://enhance-experience.com/<u>)</u> and Services and may be updated based on the evolution of the Enhance community and our Service.</p>
<p>To protect the integrity of our community, as the provider of the Service, we at Enhance reserve the right to suspend any account at any time for any conduct that we determine to be inappropriate or harmful. Such actions may include: removal of content and/or suspension of account(s).</p>
<p><strong>Breaking the Law</strong></p>
<p>You must respect all applicable local, national, and international laws while using our Services. Any content or activity featuring, encouraging, offering, or soliciting illegal activity is prohibited.</p>
<p><strong>Suspension Evasion</strong></p>
<p>All suspensions are binding until expiration or removal upon successful appeal. Any attempt to circumvent an account suspension by using other accounts, identities, or by appearing on another userâs account may also result in an additional enforcement against your accounts, up to an indefinite suspension.</p>
<p><strong>Self-Destructive Behavior</strong></p>
<p>Any activity that may endanger your life or lead to your physical harm is prohibited. This includes, but is not limited to: suicide threats, intentional physical trauma, illegal use of drugs, illegal or dangerous consumption of alcohol, and dangerous or distracted driving. We do not make exceptions for self-destructive behavior performed as a stunt or gag made in jest, or meant to entertain, when the behavior could reasonably be expected to cause physical injury.</p>
<p><strong>Violence and Threats</strong></p>
<p>Acts and threats of violence will be taken seriously and are considered zero-tolerance violations and all accounts associated with such activities may be indefinitely suspended. This includes, but is not limited to:</p>
<ul>
<li>Attempts or threats to physically harm or kill others</li>
<li>Attempts or threats to hack, DDOS, or SWAT others</li>
<li>Use of weapons to physically threaten, intimidate, harm, or kill others</li>
</ul>
<p>Enhance does not allow content that depicts, glorifies, encourages, or supports terrorism, or violent extremist actors or acts. This includes threatening to or encouraging others to commit acts that would result in serious physical harm to groups of people or significant property destruction. You may not display or link terrorist or extremist propaganda, including graphic pictures or footage of terrorist or extremist violence, even for the purposes of denouncing such content.</p>
<p><strong>Hateful Conduct and Harassment</strong></p>
<p>Hateful conduct and harassment are not allowed on Enhance. Hateful conduct is any content or activity that promotes or encourages discrimination, denigration, harassment, or violence based on the following protected characteristics: race, ethnicity, color, caste, national origin, immigration status, religion, sex, gender, gender identity, sexual orientation, disability, serious medical condition, veteran status and political affiliation. Enhance has zero tolerance for hateful conduct, we afford every user equal protections under this policy, regardless of their particular characteristics.</p>
<p>Harassment has many manifestations, including stalking, personal attacks, and promotion of physical harm. Sexual harassment, specifically, can take the form of unwelcome sexual advances and solicitations, sexual objectification, or degrading attacks relating to a personâs perceived sexual practices.</p>
<p><strong>Unauthorized Sharing of Private Information and Impersonation</strong></p>
<p>Do not invade the privacy of others. It is prohibited to share content that may reveal private personal information about individuals, or their private property, without permission. This includes but is not limited to:</p>
<ul>
<li>Sharing personally identifiable information (such as real name or location)</li>
<li>Sharing content that violates anotherâs reasonable expectation of privacy, for example using the Services video-enabled functions from a private space, without permission</li>
</ul>
<p>Content or activity meant to impersonate an individual or organization is also prohibited.</p>
<p><strong>Spam, Scams, and Other Malicious Conduct</strong></p>
<p>Any content or activity that disrupts, interrupts, harms, or otherwise violates the integrity of Enhance Services or another userâs experience or devices is prohibited. Such activity includes:</p>
<ul>
<li>Posting large amounts of repetitive, unwanted messages</li>
<li>Distributing unauthorized advertisements</li>
<li>Phishing</li>
<li>Defrauding others</li>
<li>Spreading malware or viruses</li>
<li>Misinformation</li>
<li>Tampering</li>
<li>Selling or sharing user accounts</li>
<li>Reselling Enhance Services or features</li>
<li>Defacing, or attempting to deface, website pages or other Enhance Services</li>
<li>Cheating a Enhance system<strong>&nbsp;</strong></li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Pornography, Other Sexual Content, and Potentially Obscene Content</strong></p>
<p>Depictions of sexually explicit activities or acts, including intercourse, are prohibited.&nbsp; Content that exclusively focuses on extreme or gratuitous gore and violence are also prohibited.&nbsp; Content or activities that threaten or promote sexual violence or exploitation are strictly prohibited and may be reported to law enforcement.</p>
<p><strong>Intellectual Property Rights</strong></p>
<p>You should only share content that you own, or that you otherwise have rights to or are authorized to share on Enhance. If you share content through your Enhance account that you do not own or otherwise do not have the rights to share on Enhance, you may be infringing another personâs intellectual property rights. This includes any third party content included in your content, derivative creations, or performances of othersâ copyrighted content. We encourage you to assess your content for adherence to applicable intellectual property laws and the proper application of principles such as fair use, and to secure all appropriate rights needed, before sharing your content on Enhance.</p>
<p>Any unauthorized content you share on Enhance may be subject to a takedown by the rights holder(s) to remove the infringing content from Enhance, and is a violation of these Community Guidelines. Multiple violations of our policies may lead to a permanent suspension of your account.</p>
<p>Examples of content you should not share on Enhance without permission from the copyright owners or unless otherwise permitted by law include any content, including movies, television shows, images, music or video games, you do not own or have the rights to share.</p>
<p><strong>Off-Service Conduct</strong></p>
<p>Enhance is committed to facilitating inclusive communities, which can only happen if our users feel secure and protected. In order to achieve this goal, Enhance may enforce against severe offenses committed by members of the Enhance community that occur outside of our Services, such as hate group membership, terrorist recruitment, sexual assault, and child grooming. We may investigate reports that include verifiable evidence of these behaviors and, if we are able to confirm, issue enforcements against the relevant users. We may also consider allegations of similarly severe conduct by those wishing to join the Enhance community and, if substantiated, we may terminate the account.</p>

<p><b>7. <span style="text-decoration: underline;">è²¬ä»»å¶é</span></b><b></b></p>

<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">ä¸è¿°ã®å¶éã¯ãå½è©²æå®³è³ åãå¥ç´éåãä¸æ³è¡çºï¼éå¤±ãå«ã¿ã¾ãï¼ããçãããããä»¥å¤ããçããããåãããã¾ããå½è©²æå®³è³ åãäºæ¸¬å¯è½ã§ãã£ããå¦ããã¾ãã¯ENHANCEãå½è©²æå®³è³ åã®å¯è½æ§ãç¥ãããã¦ãããå¦ãã«é¢ããããé©ç¨ããã¾ããä¸é¨ã®å¸æ³ç®¡è½åºåã¯ç¹å®ã®è²¬ä»»å¶éãè¨±å¯ãã¦ããªããããä¸è¨ã®è²¬ä»»å¶éã®ä¸é¨ã¾ãã¯å¨é¨ã¯ãå®¢ãã¾ã«ã¯é©ç¨ãããªãå¯è½æ§ãããã¾ãã</span></p>
<p><b>8. <span style="text-decoration: underline;">ææåããä»²è£ã«ããç´äºè§£æ±ºï¼æ¬æ¡ã¯ãå®¢ãã¾ã®æ¨©å©ã«å½±é¿ãã¾ãã®ã§ãæ³¨ææ·±ããèª­ã¿ãã ããã&nbsp;</span></b></p>

Conducta de odio es cualquier conducta o actividad que fomenta o alienta discriminaciÃ³n, denigraciÃ³n, acoso o violencia por razÃ³n de las siguientes condiciones protegidas: raza, origen Ã©tnico, color, casta, origen nacional, condiciÃ³n de inmigrante, religiÃ³n, sexo, gÃ©nero, identidad de gÃ©nero, orientaciÃ³n sexual, discapacidad, enfermedad grave, condiciÃ³n de veterano de guerra y afiliaciÃ³n polÃ­tica. <p dir="ltr">El acoso se manifiesta de varias formas, lo que incluye persecuciÃ³n, ataques personales y fomentar la causaciÃ³n de daÃ±os fÃ­sicos. <p dir="ltr">Derechos de propiedad intelectual</p>
<p dir="ltr">Solo debe compartir en Enhance contenidos que sean de su propiedad o que de otro modo tenga derecho o autorizaciÃ³n a compartir. <li>1.6 à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸¥à¸°à¹à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸­à¸¡à¸¹à¸¥à¸ªà¹à¸§à¸à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸¥&nbsp; à¸à¸¸à¸à¸£à¸±à¸à¸à¸£à¸²à¸à¸§à¹à¸²à¹à¸¡à¸·à¹à¸­à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸²à¸§à¸à¹à¹à¸«à¸¥à¸ à¸à¸´à¸à¸à¸±à¹à¸ à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¹à¸à¹à¹à¸à¸¡ Enhance à¸­à¸²à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸§à¸´à¸à¸µà¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¸¢à¸­à¸±à¸à¹à¸à¸¡à¸±à¸à¸´ (à¸à¸¶à¹à¸à¸£à¸§à¸¡à¸à¸¶à¸ à¸¢à¸à¸à¸±à¸§à¸­à¸¢à¹à¸²à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸ à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¹à¸¥à¸°à¹à¸§à¹à¸à¸à¸µà¸à¸­à¸) à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸¡à¸¹à¸¥à¹à¸à¸µà¹à¸¢à¸§à¸à¸±à¸à¸­à¸¸à¸à¸à¸£à¸à¹à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸¸à¸à¹à¸¥à¸°à¹à¸à¸µà¹à¸¢à¸§à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¹à¹à¸à¸¡à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸¸à¸&nbsp; à¸à¸¸à¸à¸­à¸²à¸à¸à¸°à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¹à¸«à¹à¸à¹à¸­à¸¡à¸¹à¸¥à¸à¸²à¸à¸­à¸¢à¹à¸²à¸à¹à¸à¸µà¹à¸¢à¸§à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸¸à¸à¹à¸à¸¢à¹à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸·à¹à¸­à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸²à¸§à¸à¹à¹à¸«à¸¥à¸ à¸à¸´à¸à¸à¸±à¹à¸ à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¹à¸à¹à¹à¸à¸¡ à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸­à¸£à¹à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¹à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸­à¸à¹à¸à¸¡ à¹à¸¥à¸°à¹à¸à¸¡à¸­à¸²à¸à¹à¸«à¹à¹à¸­à¸à¸²à¸ªà¸à¸¸à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸¡à¸¹à¸¥à¹à¸à¸µà¹à¸¢à¸§à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸¹à¹à¸­à¸·à¹à¸&nbsp; à¸à¹à¸­à¸¡à¸¹à¸¥à¸à¸±à¹à¸à¸«à¸¡à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¹à¸£à¸²à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸à¹à¸²à¸à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¹à¸à¸¢à¹à¸à¸µà¹à¸¢à¸§à¹à¸à¸·à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¹à¸à¸¡à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸°à¹à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸¡à¸à¹à¸¢à¸à¸²à¸¢à¸à¸§à¸²à¸¡à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸ªà¹à¸§à¸à¸à¸±à¸§à¸à¸­à¸à¹à¸£à¸²&nbsp; à¹à¸à¸¢à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸²à¸§à¸à¹à¸«à¸¥à¸ à¸à¸´à¸à¸à¸±à¹à¸ à¹à¸à¹ à¹à¸¥à¸°à¹à¸«à¹à¸à¹à¸­à¸¡à¸¹à¸¥à¹à¸à¹à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¹à¸²à¸à¹à¸à¸¡à¸à¸µà¹ à¸à¸¸à¸à¸¢à¸´à¸à¸¢à¸­à¸¡à¹à¸«à¹à¹à¸£à¸²à¸à¸³à¹à¸à¸´à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸¸à¸à¸­à¸¢à¹à¸²à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¹à¸à¸µà¹à¸¢à¸§à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸¡à¸¹à¸¥à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸¸à¸à¹à¸à¸¢à¹à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸¡à¸à¹à¸¢à¸à¸²à¸¢à¸à¸§à¸²à¸¡à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸ªà¹à¸§à¸à¸à¸±à¸§</li>
<li>1.7 à¸­à¸±à¸à¹à¸à¸&nbsp; Enhance à¸­à¸²à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸²à¹à¸¥à¸°à¹à¸«à¹à¸à¸²à¸£à¸­à¸±à¸à¹à¸à¸à¹à¸à¸¡à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸£à¸±à¹à¸à¸à¸£à¸²à¸§à¸à¸¶à¹à¸à¸­à¸¢à¸¹à¹à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸¸à¸¥à¸à¸´à¸à¸´à¸à¸à¸­à¸ Enhance à¹à¸à¹à¹à¸à¸µà¸¢à¸à¸à¸¹à¹à¹à¸à¸µà¸¢à¸§ à¸à¸¶à¹à¸à¸­à¸²à¸à¸£à¸§à¸¡à¸à¸¶à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸­à¸±à¸à¹à¸à¸£à¸ à¹à¸à¹à¹à¸à¸à¸±à¹à¸ à¹à¸à¸à¸à¹ à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¹à¹à¸à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸à¸à¸£à¹à¸­à¸à¸­à¸·à¹à¸ à¹ à¹à¸¥à¸°/à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸­à¸£à¹à¹à¸«à¸¡à¹ (à¸«à¸¡à¸²à¸¢à¸£à¸§à¸¡à¸à¸¶à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸ªà¸²à¸£à¸à¸µà¹à¹à¸à¸µà¹à¸¢à¸§à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¹à¸§à¸¢ à¹à¸£à¸µà¸¢à¸à¸£à¸§à¸¡à¹à¸à¹à¸ âà¸à¸²à¸£à¸­à¸±à¸à¹à¸à¸â)&nbsp; à¹à¸à¸¢à¹à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸¡à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸±à¹à¸à¸à¹à¸²à¸­à¸¸à¸à¸à¸£à¸à¹à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸¸à¸ à¹à¸¡à¸·à¹à¸­à¸­à¸¸à¸à¸à¸£à¸à¹à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸¸à¸à¹à¸à¸·à¹à¸­à¸¡à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸±à¸à¸­à¸´à¸à¹à¸à¸­à¸£à¹à¹à¸à¹à¸ à¹à¸¡à¹ (1) à¹à¸à¸¡à¸à¸°à¸à¸²à¸§à¸à¹à¹à¸«à¸¥à¸à¹à¸¥à¸°à¸à¸´à¸à¸à¸±à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸­à¸±à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¸¡à¸µà¸­à¸¢à¸¹à¹à¸à¸±à¹à¸à¸«à¸¡à¸à¹à¸à¸¢à¸­à¸±à¸à¹à¸à¸¡à¸±à¸à¸´à¹à¸­à¸ à¸à¹ (2) à¸à¸¸à¸à¸­à¸²à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸£à¸±à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸·à¸­à¸à¸à¸­à¸à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¹à¸à¸·à¸­à¸à¹à¸«à¹à¸à¸²à¸§à¸à¹à¹à¸«à¸¥à¸à¹à¸¥à¸°à¸à¸´à¸à¸à¸±à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸­à¸±à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¸¡à¸µà¸­à¸¢à¸¹à¹à¸à¸±à¹à¸à¸«à¸¡à¸&nbsp; <li><span style="font-weight: 400;">(3) à¸à¹à¸¢à¸à¸²à¸¢à¸à¸¹à¹à¸à¸³à¸à¸²à¸£à¸¥à¸°à¹à¸¡à¸´à¸à¸à¹à¸³</span><span style="font-weight: 400;">&nbsp; à¸à¹à¸¢à¸à¸²à¸¢à¸à¸£à¸±à¸à¸¢à¹à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸­à¸ Enhance à¸¡à¸µà¹à¸à¸·à¹à¸­ (1) à¸¥à¸à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸¢à¸à¹à¸¥à¸´à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¹à¸²à¸à¸¶à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸¡à¸¹à¸¥à¸à¸µà¹ Enhance à¹à¸à¸·à¹à¸­à¹à¸à¸¢à¸ªà¸¸à¸à¸£à¸´à¸ à¹à¸à¸¢à¹à¸à¹à¸£à¸±à¸à¸à¸³à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¹à¸²à¸§à¸à¸²à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸²à¸à¸­à¸à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¸´à¹à¸à¸à¸£à¸±à¸à¸¢à¹à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸²à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¸±à¸§à¹à¸à¸à¸à¸­à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸²à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸¥à¹à¸²à¸§ à¸§à¹à¸²à¸¡à¸µà¸à¸²à¸£à¸¥à¸°à¹à¸¡à¸´à¸à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¸´à¹à¸à¸à¸£à¸±à¸à¸¢à¹à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸¥à¸ à¸²à¸¢à¸à¸­à¸à¹à¸à¸¢à¸à¸³à¹à¸«à¹à¸à¸£à¹à¸­à¸¡à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¹à¸²à¸à¹à¸à¸¡ à¹à¸¥à¸° (2) à¹à¸à¸ªà¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¹à¸à¸µà¹à¹à¸«à¸¡à¸²à¸°à¸ªà¸¡ à¹à¸à¸·à¹à¸­à¸¢à¸à¹à¸¥à¸´à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸µà¸à¸­à¸à¹à¸¥à¸°à¸à¸¥à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¹à¸²à¸à¸¶à¸à¹à¸à¸¡à¹à¸à¸¢à¸à¸¹à¹à¹à¸à¹à¹à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸³à¸à¸²à¸£à¸¥à¸°à¹à¸¡à¸´à¸à¸¥à¸´à¸à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¸´à¹à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¸´à¹à¸à¸à¸£à¸±à¸à¸¢à¹à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸¹à¹à¸­à¸·à¹à¸à¸­à¸¢à¹à¸²à¸à¸à¹à¸³ à¹ à¹à¸¥à¸°à¸£à¹à¸²à¸¢à¹à¸£à¸</span></li>

<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Enhance à¹à¸«à¹à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¸´à¹à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¹à¸à¸¡à¸à¸µà¹à¸­à¸²à¸à¸à¸³à¹à¸«à¹à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸²à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸²à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸ªà¹à¸à¸£à¹à¸à¸­à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¹à¸à¸´à¸¥ à¹à¸à¸¥à¸¢à¹à¸ªà¹à¸à¸£à¹à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸¹à¹à¸à¸´à¸¥ à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸³à¸«à¸à¹à¸²à¸¢à¸­à¸·à¹à¸ (âà¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸³à¸«à¸à¹à¸²à¸¢â)&nbsp; à¸«à¸²à¸à¸à¸¸à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸£à¸±à¸à¹à¸à¸¡à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸¥à¹à¸²à¸§à¸à¹à¸²à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸³à¸«à¸à¹à¸²à¸¢ à¸à¸¸à¸à¸­à¸²à¸à¸­à¸¢à¸¹à¹à¸ à¸²à¸¢à¹à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸³à¸«à¸à¸à¹à¸à¸´à¹à¸¡à¹à¸à¸´à¸¡à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸³à¸«à¸à¹à¸²à¸¢à¸à¸±à¹à¸ à¹&nbsp; à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸³à¸à¸¶à¹à¸à¸£à¸°à¸«à¸§à¹à¸²à¸à¸à¸¸à¸à¹à¸¥à¸°à¹à¸£à¸²à¹à¸à¹à¸²à¸à¸±à¹à¸ à¹à¸à¸¢à¸¡à¸´à¹à¸à¹à¸¡à¸µà¸à¸¥à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸³à¸«à¸à¹à¸²à¸¢&nbsp; à¸à¸£à¸²à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸²à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸¸à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸¥à¸´à¸à¸ à¸±à¸à¸à¹à¹à¸¥à¸°à¸à¸£à¸´à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸¥à¸ à¸²à¸¢à¸à¸­à¸à¸­à¸·à¹à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸¢à¹à¸à¸µà¹à¸¢à¸§à¹à¸à¸·à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸²à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¸´à¹à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¹à¸à¸¡à¸à¸­à¸à¹à¸£à¸² à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸à¸¥à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸°à¸à¸à¸´à¸à¸±à¸à¸´à¸à¸²à¸¡à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸³à¸«à¸à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸±à¹à¸à¸«à¸¡à¸à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¸à¹à¸ à¹ à¸ªà¸³à¸«à¸£à¸±à¸à¸à¸¥à¸´à¸à¸ à¸±à¸à¸à¹à¹à¸¥à¸°à¸à¸£à¸´à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸¥à¸ à¸²à¸¢à¸à¸­à¸</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">à¸ªà¸³à¸«à¸£à¸±à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¸´à¹à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¹à¸à¸¡à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸³à¹à¸«à¹à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸²à¸à¹à¸à¹à¹à¸à¸·à¹à¸­à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸¸à¸à¹à¸à¸¢à¹à¸à¸µà¹à¸¢à¸§à¹à¸à¸·à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸¥à¸´à¸à¸ à¸±à¸à¸à¹à¸ à¸²à¸¢à¹à¸à¹à¹à¸à¸£à¸à¸à¹à¹à¸­à¸à¹à¸à¸´à¸¥ (à¹à¸à¹à¸ à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¸´à¹à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¹à¸à¸¡ â</span><b>à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¸´à¹à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸ªà¸³à¸«à¸£à¸±à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¹à¸à¸´à¸¥</b><span style="font-weight: 400;">â) à¸à¸­à¸à¹à¸«à¸à¸·à¸­à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸³à¸«à¸à¸à¹à¸¥à¸°à¹à¸à¸·à¹à¸­à¸à¹à¸à¸­à¸·à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¸£à¸°à¸à¸¸à¹à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¸à¸à¸µà¹ à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸³à¸«à¸à¸à¹à¸¥à¸°à¹à¸à¸·à¹à¸­à¸à¹à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¹à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸°à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸±à¸</span></p>

<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Enhance à¹à¸¥à¸°à¸à¸¸à¸à¸£à¸±à¸à¸à¸£à¸²à¸à¸§à¹à¸²à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¸ªà¸£à¸¸à¸à¸£à¸°à¸«à¸§à¹à¸²à¸ Enhance à¹à¸¥à¸°à¸à¸¸à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸²à¸à¸±à¹à¸ à¹à¸à¸¢à¹à¸¡à¹à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸±à¸ Apple Inc. (â</span><b>à¹à¸­à¸à¹à¸à¸´à¸¥</b><span style="font-weight: 400;">â) à¹à¸¥à¸°à¸£à¸°à¸«à¸§à¹à¸²à¸ Enhance à¹à¸¥à¸°à¹à¸­à¸à¹à¸à¸´à¸¥ Enhance à¸à¸°à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸¹à¹à¸£à¸±à¸à¸à¸´à¸à¸à¸­à¸à¹à¸à¹à¹à¸à¸µà¸¢à¸à¸à¸¹à¹à¹à¸à¸µà¸¢à¸§à¸à¹à¸­à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¸´à¹à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸ªà¸³à¸«à¸£à¸±à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¹à¸à¸´à¸¥à¹à¸¥à¸°à¹à¸à¸·à¹à¸­à¸«à¸²à¸à¸­à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¸´à¹à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸¥à¹à¸²à¸§</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">à¸à¸¸à¸à¹à¸¡à¹à¸­à¸²à¸à¹à¸à¹à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¸´à¹à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸ªà¸³à¸«à¸£à¸±à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¹à¸à¸´à¸¥à¹à¸à¸¢à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸¥à¸°à¹à¸¡à¸´à¸à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¹à¸¡à¹à¸ªà¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸£à¸°à¹à¸à¸µà¸¢à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸³à¸«à¸à¸à¸ªà¸³à¸«à¸£à¸±à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¸´à¹à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸ªà¸³à¸«à¸£à¸±à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¹à¸à¸´à¸¥à¸ à¸²à¸¢à¹à¸ à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¹à¸à¸¢à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸³à¸«à¸à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸«à¹à¸à¸£à¸´à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸­à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸ªà¹à¸à¸£à¹</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¸´à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸¸à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¹à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¸´à¹à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸ªà¸³à¸«à¸£à¸±à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¹à¸à¸´à¸¥à¹à¸à¹à¸£à¸±à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸³à¸à¸±à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¸´à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¹à¸¡à¹à¸ªà¸²à¸¡à¸²à¸£à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¹à¸à¹à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¹à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¸´à¹à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸ªà¸³à¸«à¸£à¸±à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¹à¸à¸´à¸¥à¹à¸à¸à¸¥à¸´à¸à¸ à¸±à¸à¸à¹à¸£à¸°à¸à¸ iOS à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸£à¸­à¸à¸à¸£à¸­à¸à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¸§à¸à¸à¸¸à¸¡ à¸à¸²à¸¡à¸à¸µà¹à¹à¸à¹à¸£à¸±à¸à¸­à¸à¸¸à¸à¸²à¸à¹à¸à¸¢à¸£à¸°à¹à¸à¸µà¸¢à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸³à¸«à¸à¸à¹à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸³à¸«à¸à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸«à¹à¸à¸£à¸´à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸­à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸ªà¹à¸à¸£à¹</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">à¹à¸­à¸à¹à¸à¸´à¸¥à¹à¸¡à¹à¸¡à¸µà¸ à¸²à¸£à¸°à¸«à¸à¹à¸²à¸à¸µà¹à¹à¸ à¹ à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸«à¹à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸³à¸£à¸¸à¸à¸£à¸±à¸à¸©à¸²à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¸£à¸´à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¹à¸§à¸¢à¹à¸«à¸¥à¸·à¸­à¹à¸à¸ªà¹à¸§à¸à¸à¸­à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¸´à¹à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸ªà¸³à¸«à¸£à¸±à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¹à¸à¸´à¸¥</span></li>

<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Enhance à¹à¸¥à¸°à¸à¸¸à¸à¸£à¸±à¸à¸à¸£à¸²à¸à¸§à¹à¸² Enhance à¸¡à¸´à¹à¸à¹à¹à¸­à¸à¹à¸à¸´à¸¥ à¸à¸°à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸¹à¹à¸£à¸±à¸à¸à¸´à¸à¸à¸­à¸à¹à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¹à¸£à¸µà¸¢à¸à¸£à¹à¸­à¸à¹à¸ à¹ à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸¸à¸à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸¥à¸ à¸²à¸¢à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¹à¸à¸µà¹à¸¢à¸§à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¸´à¹à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸ªà¸³à¸«à¸£à¸±à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¹à¸à¸´à¸¥à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸£à¸­à¸à¸à¸£à¸­à¸à¹à¸¥à¸°/à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¹à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¸´à¹à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸ªà¸³à¸«à¸£à¸±à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¹à¸à¸´à¸¥à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸¸à¸ à¸à¸¶à¹à¸à¸£à¸§à¸¡à¸à¸¶à¸à¹à¸à¹à¹à¸¡à¹à¸à¸³à¸à¸±à¸à¹à¸à¸µà¸¢à¸ (1) à¸à¹à¸­à¹à¸£à¸µà¸¢à¸à¸£à¹à¸­à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸§à¸²à¸¡à¸£à¸±à¸à¸à¸´à¸à¸à¸¥à¸´à¸à¸ à¸±à¸à¸à¹ (2) à¸à¹à¸­à¹à¸£à¸µà¸¢à¸à¸£à¹à¸­à¸à¹à¸ à¹ à¸§à¹à¸²à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¸´à¹à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸ªà¸³à¸«à¸£à¸±à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¹à¸à¸´à¸¥à¹à¸¡à¹à¸à¸à¸´à¸à¸±à¸à¸´à¸à¸²à¸¡à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸³à¸«à¸à¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸à¸«à¸¡à¸²à¸¢à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¸à¸£à¸°à¹à¸à¸µà¸¢à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸±à¸ à¹à¸¥à¸° (3) à¸à¹à¸­à¹à¸£à¸µà¸¢à¸à¸£à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¸¡à¸µà¸à¸¶à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸¸à¹à¸¡à¸à¸£à¸­à¸à¸à¸¹à¹à¸à¸£à¸´à¹à¸ à¸à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸´à¸à¸à¸«à¸¡à¸²à¸¢à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸¥à¹à¸²à¸¢à¸à¸¥à¸¶à¸</span></li>

<ul>
<li><span style="font-weight: 400;">4.1 à¸à¸²à¸£à¸­à¸à¸¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸³à¸£à¸°à¹à¸à¸´à¸</span><span style="font-weight: 400;">&nbsp; à¹à¸à¸¡à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸ªà¹à¸§à¸à¸­à¸²à¸à¹à¸«à¹à¸à¸¸à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸²à¸à¹à¸à¹à¹à¸¡à¸·à¹à¸­à¸¡à¸µà¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¹à¸²à¸¢à¸à¹à¸²à¸à¸£à¸£à¸¡à¹à¸à¸µà¸¢à¸¡&nbsp; à¹à¸¡à¸·à¹à¸­à¸à¸¸à¸à¹à¸«à¹à¸à¹à¸­à¸¡à¸¹à¸¥à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸³à¸£à¸°à¹à¸à¸´à¸à¹à¸à¹ Enhance à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸¹à¹à¸à¸£à¸°à¸¡à¸§à¸¥à¸à¸¥à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸³à¸£à¸°à¹à¸à¸´à¸à¸à¸­à¸ Enhance à¸£à¸²à¸¢à¸«à¸à¸¶à¹à¸ à¸à¸¸à¸à¸£à¸±à¸à¸£à¸­à¸à¹à¸à¹ Enhance à¸§à¹à¸²à¸à¸¸à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸¹à¹à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸µà¹à¹à¸à¹à¸£à¸±à¸à¸­à¸à¸¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸£ à¸£à¸«à¸±à¸ª PIN à¸à¸¸à¸à¹à¸à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸µà¸à¸µà¹à¹à¸à¸µà¹à¸¢à¸§à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸ªà¸·à¹à¸­à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸³à¸£à¸°à¹à¸à¸´à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸¥à¹à¸²à¸§ à¹à¸¥à¸°à¸à¸¸à¸à¸­à¸à¸¸à¸à¸²à¸à¹à¸«à¹ Enhance à¹à¸£à¸µà¸¢à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸à¹à¸²à¹à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸²à¸¢à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸£à¹à¸à¸£à¸à¸´à¸à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸ªà¸·à¹à¸­à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸³à¸£à¸°à¹à¸à¸´à¸à¸­à¸·à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸ªà¸³à¸«à¸£à¸±à¸à¹à¸à¸´à¸à¸à¸¸à¸à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¹à¸²à¸à¸£à¸£à¸¡à¹à¸à¸µà¸¢à¸¡à¸­à¸·à¹à¸à¹à¸ (à¸£à¸§à¸¡à¸à¸¶à¸à¸à¹à¸²à¸à¸£à¸£à¸¡à¹à¸à¸µà¸¢à¸¡à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸³à¸à¸¸à¸£à¸à¸£à¸£à¸¡à¹à¸¥à¸°à¸à¸±à¸à¸£à¹à¸à¸£à¸à¸´à¸) à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸³à¹à¸«à¹à¸¡à¸µà¸à¸¶à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸¢à¹à¸à¸µà¹à¸¢à¸§à¹à¸à¸·à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¹à¸à¸¡&nbsp; Enhance à¸­à¸²à¸à¹à¸«à¹à¸à¸¸à¸à¸£à¸°à¸à¸¸à¸à¸µà¹à¸­à¸¢à¸¹à¹à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¹à¸­à¸¡à¸¹à¸¥à¸­à¸·à¹à¸ à¹ à¹à¸à¸·à¹à¸­à¹à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸¡à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸¹à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸²à¸¡à¸à¸à¸«à¸¡à¸²à¸¢à¸ à¸²à¸©à¸µà¸à¸µà¹à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸±à¸&nbsp; à¸«à¸²à¸à¸£à¸²à¸¢à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸·à¹à¸­à¹à¸à¸­à¸¢à¸¹à¹à¸ à¸²à¸¢à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸£à¸°à¹à¸ à¸à¸à¸­à¸à¸ à¸²à¸©à¸µà¸¡à¸¹à¸¥à¸à¹à¸²à¹à¸à¸´à¹à¸¡ (VAT) à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¹à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸ à¸²à¸©à¸µà¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸²à¸¢ à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸±à¹à¸ Enhance à¸­à¸²à¸à¸à¸°à¹à¸£à¸µà¸¢à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸à¹à¸²à¹à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸²à¸¢à¸à¸¸à¸à¸ªà¸³à¸«à¸£à¸±à¸à¸ à¸²à¸©à¸µà¹à¸«à¸¥à¹à¸²à¸à¸±à¹à¸à¸à¹à¸§à¸¢ à¸£à¸§à¸¡à¸à¸±à¹à¸à¸à¹à¸²à¸à¸£à¸£à¸¡à¹à¸à¸µà¸¢à¸¡à¸­à¸·à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸±à¸</span></li>
<li>4.2 à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸·à¹à¸­à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¹à¸²à¸à¸´à¸à¸´à¸à¸±à¸¥&nbsp; âà¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¹à¸²à¸à¸´à¸à¸´à¸à¸±à¸¥â à¸«à¸¡à¸²à¸¢à¸à¸¶à¸à¹à¸à¸·à¹à¸­à¸«à¸² (à¸£à¸§à¸¡à¸à¸¶à¸à¹à¸à¹à¹à¸¡à¹à¸à¸³à¸à¸±à¸à¹à¸à¸µà¸¢à¸à¸ªà¸à¸¸à¸¥à¹à¸à¸´à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸¡) à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸·à¹à¸­à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¹à¸à¹à¸£à¸±à¸à¹à¸à¸·à¹à¸­à¹à¸à¹à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸¡à¸à¹à¸²à¸à¸à¸¥à¹à¸à¸¥à¸à¸µà¹à¹à¸£à¸²à¸à¸³à¹à¸«à¹à¸¡à¸µà¸à¸¶à¹à¸&nbsp; à¹à¸à¸¢à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸·à¹à¸­à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¹à¸à¹à¸£à¸±à¸à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¹à¸²à¸à¸´à¸à¸´à¸à¸±à¸¥à¸à¹à¸§à¸¢à¸§à¸´à¸à¸µà¸­à¸·à¹à¸à¹à¸ à¸à¸¸à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸£à¸±à¸à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¸´à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸³à¸à¸±à¸à¹à¸¥à¸°à¹à¸¡à¹à¸à¸¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸ (à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¹à¸à¹à¸£à¸°à¸à¸¸à¹à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¸à¸à¸µà¹) à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¹à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¹à¸²à¸à¸´à¸à¸´à¸à¸±à¸¥à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸¥à¹à¸²à¸§à¸ à¸²à¸¢à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸¡&nbsp; à¸à¸­à¸à¹à¸«à¸à¸·à¸­à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¸´à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸³à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸µà¹ à¸à¸¸à¸à¹à¸¡à¹à¸¡à¸µà¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¸´à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¸£à¸£à¸¡à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¸´à¹à¸­à¸·à¹à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¹à¸­à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¹à¸²à¸à¸´à¸à¸´à¸à¸±à¸¥&nbsp; à¸à¸±à¹à¸à¸à¸µà¹ à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¹à¸²à¸à¸´à¸à¸´à¸à¸±à¸¥à¹à¸¡à¹à¸ªà¸²à¸¡à¸²à¸£à¸à¸à¸³à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸¢à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¹à¸­à¸à¹à¸«à¹à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸¥à¸ à¸²à¸¢à¸à¸­à¸à¹à¸à¹ (à¹à¸§à¹à¸à¹à¸ªà¸µà¸¢à¹à¸à¹à¸§à¹à¸²à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¹à¸à¹à¸£à¸±à¸à¸­à¸à¸¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸ à¸²à¸¢à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸¡) à¹à¸¥à¸°à¹à¸¡à¹à¸ªà¸²à¸¡à¸²à¸£à¸à¹à¸¥à¸à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¹à¸à¸¥à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸´à¸à¸ªà¸à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¸±à¹à¸§à¹à¸à¸´à¸à¸ªà¸³à¸«à¸£à¸±à¸à¸à¸³à¸£à¸°à¸«à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸²à¸¡à¸à¸à¸«à¸¡à¸²à¸¢à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¹à¸¥à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¹à¸²à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¸£à¸´à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¸à¸­à¸à¹à¸à¸¡&nbsp; à¸«à¸²à¸à¸à¸¸à¸à¸­à¸²à¸¨à¸±à¸¢à¸­à¸¢à¸¹à¹à¹à¸à¸ªà¸«à¸ à¸²à¸à¸¢à¸¸à¹à¸£à¸ à¸à¸¸à¸à¸¡à¸µà¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¸´à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸£à¸°à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸·à¹à¸­à¸à¸²à¸à¹à¸à¸¥ à¸­à¸¢à¹à¸²à¸à¹à¸£à¸à¹à¸à¸µ à¹à¸à¸£à¸à¸à¸£à¸²à¸à¸§à¹à¸²à¹à¸¡à¸·à¹à¸­à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸·à¹à¸­à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¸´à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸²à¸à¹à¸à¸·à¹à¸­à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸²à¸à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¹à¸²à¹à¸ªà¸¡à¸·à¸­à¸ (Virtual Goods) à¸à¸²à¸à¹à¸£à¸² à¸à¸¸à¸à¸£à¸±à¸à¸à¸£à¸²à¸à¹à¸¥à¸°à¸à¸à¸¥à¸à¸§à¹à¸²à¹à¸£à¸²à¸à¸°à¹à¸£à¸´à¹à¸¡à¹à¸«à¹à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¹à¸²à¹à¸ªà¸¡à¸·à¸­à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸µà¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸·à¹à¸­à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸¸à¸à¹à¸ªà¸£à¹à¸à¸ªà¸´à¹à¸à¹à¸¥à¸°à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸¶à¸à¸ªà¸¹à¸à¹à¸ªà¸µà¸¢à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¸´à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸­à¸à¹à¸¡à¸·à¹à¸­à¸à¸¶à¸à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸µà¹&nbsp; à¹à¸à¸¢à¸¡à¸µà¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸£à¸°à¸ªà¸à¸à¹à¹à¸à¸·à¹à¸­à¸«à¸¡à¸§à¸à¸à¸µà¹ âà¸£à¸²à¸¢à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸·à¹à¸­â à¸à¸°à¹à¸ªà¸£à¹à¸à¸ªà¸´à¹à¸ à¸ à¹à¸§à¸¥à¸²à¸à¸µà¹à¹à¸à¸´à¸£à¹à¸à¹à¸§à¸­à¸£à¹à¸à¸­à¸à¹à¸£à¸²à¸¢à¸·à¸à¸¢à¸±à¸à¸£à¸²à¸¢à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸·à¹à¸­à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸¸à¸à¹à¸¥à¸°à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¹à¸²à¹à¸ªà¸¡à¸·à¸­à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸£à¸±à¸à¹à¸à¸£à¸à¸´à¸à¹à¸à¸¢à¸±à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸µà¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸à¹à¸à¸´à¸£à¹à¸à¹à¸§à¸­à¸£à¹à¸à¸­à¸à¹à¸£à¸²</li>
<li>4.3 à¹à¸¡à¹à¸¡à¸µà¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸·à¸à¹à¸à¸´à¸&nbsp; à¸£à¸²à¸¢à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸·à¹à¸­à¸à¸¸à¸à¸£à¸²à¸¢à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸³à¹à¸à¸´à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¹à¸²à¸à¹à¸à¸¡à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¸ªà¸´à¹à¸à¸ªà¸¸à¸à¹à¸¥à¸°à¹à¸¡à¹à¸ªà¸²à¸¡à¸²à¸£à¸à¸à¸·à¸à¹à¸à¸´à¸à¹à¸à¹</li>
<li>4.4 à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸³à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¹à¸à¸µà¹à¸¢à¸§à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¹à¸²à¸à¸´à¸à¸´à¸à¸±à¸¥&nbsp; Enhance à¸­à¸²à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸²à¸£ à¸§à¸²à¸à¸£à¸°à¹à¸à¸µà¸¢à¸ à¸à¸§à¸à¸à¸¸à¸¡ à¹à¸à¹à¹à¸ à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¸³à¸à¸±à¸à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¹à¸²à¹à¸ªà¸¡à¸·à¸­à¸à¹à¸¡à¸·à¹à¸­à¹à¸à¸à¹à¹à¸à¹ à¹à¸à¸¢à¸¡à¸µà¸à¸³à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¹à¸²à¸§à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¹à¸¡à¹à¸¡à¸µà¸à¹à¹à¸à¹&nbsp; Enhance à¸à¸°à¹à¸¡à¹à¸¡à¸µà¸à¸§à¸²à¸¡à¸£à¸±à¸à¸à¸´à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸¸à¸à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸¥à¸ à¸²à¸¢à¸à¸­à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸£à¸à¸µà¸à¸µà¹ Enhance à¹à¸à¹à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¸´à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸¥à¹à¸²à¸§&nbsp; à¸«à¹à¸²à¸¡à¹à¸«à¹à¸¡à¸µà¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸­à¸à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¹à¸²à¹à¸ªà¸¡à¸·à¸­à¸à¹à¸§à¹à¸à¹à¸ªà¸µà¸¢à¹à¸à¹à¸§à¹à¸² Enhance à¸à¸°à¹à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸­à¸¢à¹à¸²à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸&nbsp; à¸à¸­à¸à¹à¸«à¸à¸·à¸­à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸£à¸à¸µà¸à¸µà¹à¹à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸­à¸¢à¹à¸²à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸ à¸²à¸¢à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸¡ à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸°à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¹à¸¡à¹à¸à¸²à¸¢ à¹à¸¥à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸´à¸ à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¹à¸­à¸à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¹à¸²à¹à¸ªà¸¡à¸·à¸­à¸à¹à¸«à¹à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸¥à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸«à¸à¹à¸§à¸¢à¸à¸²à¸à¹à¸ à¸£à¸§à¸¡à¸à¸¶à¸à¹à¸à¹à¹à¸¡à¹à¸à¸³à¸à¸±à¸à¹à¸à¸µà¸¢à¸ Enhance à¸à¸¹à¹à¹à¸à¹à¸­à¸·à¹à¸ à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸¥à¸ à¸²à¸¢à¸à¸­à¸à¹à¸</li>

<li><span style="font-weight: 400;">5.1 à¸£à¸°à¸¢à¸°à¹à¸§à¸¥à¸²</span><span style="font-weight: 400;">&nbsp; à¸£à¸°à¸¢à¸°à¹à¸§à¸¥à¸²à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¸à¹à¸£à¸´à¹à¸¡à¸à¸¶à¹à¸à¹à¸¡à¸·à¹à¸­à¸à¸¸à¸à¹à¸à¹à¹à¸à¸¡à¹à¸¥à¸°à¸à¸°à¸¡à¸µà¸à¸¥à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸­à¹à¸à¸à¸à¸à¸£à¸°à¸à¸±à¹à¸à¸à¸¸à¸à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­ Enhance à¸à¸­à¸à¹à¸¥à¸´à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¸à¸à¸²à¸¡à¸à¸µà¹à¹à¸à¹à¸£à¸°à¸à¸¸à¹à¸à¸«à¸¡à¸§à¸ 5 à¸à¸µà¹</span></li>
<li>5.2 à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸­à¸à¹à¸¥à¸´à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¸à¹à¸à¸¢à¸à¸¸à¸&nbsp; à¸à¸¸à¸à¸­à¸²à¸à¸à¸­à¸à¹à¸¥à¸´à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¸à¹à¸à¹à¹à¸à¸¢à¸¥à¸à¹à¸à¸¡à¹à¸¥à¸°à¸ªà¸³à¹à¸à¸²à¹à¸à¸¡à¸à¸±à¹à¸à¸«à¸¡à¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸­à¸¸à¸à¸à¸£à¸à¹à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸¸à¸</li>
<li>5.3 à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸­à¸à¹à¸¥à¸´à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¸à¹à¸à¸¢ Enhance&nbsp; Enhance à¸­à¸²à¸à¸à¸­à¸à¹à¸¥à¸´à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¹à¸¡à¸·à¹à¸­à¹à¸à¸à¹à¹à¸à¹à¹à¸à¸¢à¹à¸¡à¹à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸¡à¸µà¸à¸³à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¹à¸²à¸§à¸«à¸²à¸ Enhance à¸¢à¸¸à¸à¸´à¹à¸«à¹à¸à¸²à¸£à¸ªà¸à¸±à¸à¸ªà¸à¸¸à¸à¹à¸à¸¡à¹à¸¥à¹à¸§ à¸à¸¶à¹à¸ Enhance à¸­à¸²à¸à¸à¸³à¹à¸à¸´à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸¥à¹à¸²à¸§à¸à¸µà¹à¹à¸à¸¢à¸à¸¶à¹à¸à¸­à¸¢à¸¹à¹à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸¸à¸¥à¸à¸´à¸à¸´à¸à¸à¸­à¸ Enhance à¹à¸à¹à¹à¸à¸µà¸¢à¸à¸à¸¹à¹à¹à¸à¸µà¸¢à¸§&nbsp; à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸µà¹ à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸°à¸ªà¸´à¹à¸à¸ªà¸¸à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¸¥à¸°à¹à¸à¸¢à¸­à¸±à¸à¹à¸à¸¡à¸±à¸à¸´à¹à¸à¸¢à¹à¸¡à¹à¸¡à¸µà¸à¸³à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¹à¸²à¸§à¸«à¸²à¸à¸à¸¸à¸à¸¥à¸°à¹à¸¡à¸´à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸³à¸«à¸à¸à¹à¸¥à¸°à¹à¸à¸·à¹à¸­à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸ à¹ à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¸à¸à¸µà¹</li>
<li>5.4 à¸à¸¥à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸­à¸à¹à¸¥à¸´à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¸&nbsp; à¹à¸¡à¸·à¹à¸­à¸à¸­à¸à¹à¸¥à¸´à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¸ à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¸´à¸à¸±à¹à¸à¸«à¸¡à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸¸à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸£à¸±à¸à¸à¸²à¸¡à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸°à¸ªà¸´à¹à¸à¸ªà¸¸à¸à¹à¸à¸à¹à¸§à¸¢ à¹à¸¥à¸°à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸«à¸¢à¸¸à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¹à¹à¸à¸¡à¸à¸±à¹à¸à¸«à¸¡à¸à¹à¸¥à¸°à¸¥à¸à¸ªà¸³à¹à¸à¸²à¸à¸­à¸à¹à¸à¸¡à¸à¸±à¹à¸à¸«à¸¡à¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸­à¸¸à¸à¸à¸£à¸à¹à¹à¸¥à¸°à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸µà¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸¸à¸&nbsp; à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸­à¸à¹à¸¥à¸´à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¸à¸à¸°à¹à¸¡à¹à¸à¸³à¸à¸±à¸à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¸´à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸¢à¸µà¸¢à¸§à¸¢à¸²à¹à¸ à¹ à¸à¸­à¸ Enhance à¸à¸²à¸¡à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸à¸«à¸¡à¸²à¸¢à¸à¸³à¸«à¸à¸</li>

<p>6. à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸³à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸§à¸²à¸¡à¸£à¸±à¸à¸à¸´à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸£à¸±à¸à¸à¸£à¸°à¸à¸±à¸</p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">à¹à¸à¸¡à¸¡à¸µà¹à¸«à¹à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸¹à¹à¸£à¸±à¸à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¸´à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸µà¹ âà¸à¸²à¸¡à¸ªà¸ à¸²à¸à¸à¸£à¸´à¸â à¹à¸¥à¸°à¸¡à¸µà¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸à¸£à¹à¸­à¸à¹à¸¥à¸°à¸à¸³à¸«à¸à¸´à¹à¸à¸¢à¹à¸¡à¹à¸¡à¸µà¸à¸²à¸£à¸£à¸±à¸à¸à¸£à¸°à¸à¸±à¸à¹à¸à¸£à¸¹à¸à¹à¸à¸à¹à¸à¸à¹à¸à¸²à¸¡&nbsp; à¸à¸²à¸¡à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸à¸«à¸¡à¸²à¸¢à¸à¸µà¹à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸³à¸«à¸à¸ Enhance à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸¡à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸à¹à¸¥à¸°à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸¡à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸£à¸´à¸©à¸±à¸à¸£à¹à¸§à¸¡à¹à¸¥à¸°à¸à¸¹à¹à¹à¸«à¹à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¸´à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸²à¸à¹à¸¥à¸°à¸à¸¹à¹à¹à¸«à¹à¸à¸£à¸´à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸²à¸¡à¸¥à¸³à¸à¸±à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸´à¹à¸ªà¸à¸à¸§à¸²à¸¡à¸£à¸±à¸à¸à¸´à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸£à¸±à¸à¸à¸£à¸°à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸±à¹à¸à¸«à¸¡à¸à¹à¸à¸¢à¸à¸±à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸ à¹à¸¡à¹à¸§à¹à¸²à¸à¸°à¹à¸à¸¢à¸à¸±à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸ à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸±à¸¢ à¸à¸²à¸¡à¸à¸à¸«à¸¡à¸²à¸¢ à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¹à¸à¸¢à¸à¸£à¸°à¸à¸²à¸£à¸­à¸·à¹à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸ªà¹à¸§à¸à¸à¸­à¸à¹à¸à¸¡ à¸£à¸§à¸¡à¸à¸¶à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸£à¸±à¸à¸à¸£à¸°à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸§à¸²à¸¡à¸ªà¸²à¸¡à¸²à¸£à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¹à¸²à¸à¸²à¸¢à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸µà¹à¸£à¸°à¸à¸¸à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸±à¸¢ à¸à¸§à¸²à¸¡à¹à¸«à¸¡à¸²à¸°à¸ªà¸¡à¸ªà¸³à¸«à¸£à¸±à¸à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸£à¸°à¸ªà¸à¸à¹à¸à¸£à¸°à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¸à¸£à¸°à¸à¸²à¸£à¸«à¸à¸¶à¹à¸ à¸à¸£à¸£à¸¡à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¸´à¹ à¹à¸¥à¸°à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸¡à¹à¸¥à¸°à¹à¸¡à¸´à¸à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¸´ à¹à¸¥à¸°à¸à¸²à¸£à¸£à¸±à¸à¸à¸£à¸°à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¸­à¸²à¸à¸¡à¸µà¸à¸¶à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸·à¹à¸­à¸à¸²à¸¢ à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸³à¹à¸à¸´à¸à¸à¸²à¸ à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¹ à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸à¸´à¸à¸±à¸à¸´à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¹à¸²&nbsp; à¹à¸à¸¢à¹à¸¡à¹à¸à¸³à¸à¸±à¸à¹à¸à¹à¹à¸à¸µà¸¢à¸à¸à¹à¸²à¸à¸à¹à¸ Enhance à¸¢à¸±à¸à¹à¸¡à¹à¹à¸«à¹à¸à¸²à¸£à¸£à¸±à¸à¸à¸£à¸°à¸à¸±à¸à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸¡à¸µà¸ à¸²à¸£à¸°à¸«à¸à¹à¸²à¸à¸µà¹ à¹à¸¥à¸°à¹à¸¡à¹à¹à¸«à¹à¸à¸²à¸£à¸£à¸±à¸à¸£à¸­à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸­à¸¢à¹à¸²à¸à¹à¸à¸§à¹à¸²à¹à¸à¸¡à¸à¸°à¹à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸¡à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸³à¸«à¸à¸à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸¸à¸ à¸à¸£à¸£à¸¥à¸¸à¸à¸¥à¸¥à¸±à¸à¸à¹à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸£à¸°à¸ªà¸à¸à¹ à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¹à¸§à¸¢à¸à¸±à¸à¹à¸à¹ à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¸³à¸à¸²à¸à¸£à¹à¸§à¸¡à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¹à¹à¸§à¸£à¹ à¹à¸à¸¡ à¸£à¸°à¸à¸ à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¸£à¸´à¸à¸²à¸£à¸­à¸·à¹à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸à¹ à¸à¸à¸´à¸à¸±à¸à¸´à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¸¢à¹à¸¡à¹à¸¡à¸µà¸à¸²à¸£à¸ªà¸°à¸à¸¸à¸ à¹à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸¡à¸¡à¸²à¸à¸£à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸³à¹à¸à¸´à¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¸§à¸²à¸¡à¸à¹à¸²à¹à¸à¸·à¹à¸­à¸à¸·à¸­à¹à¸ à¹ à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¸£à¸²à¸¨à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸´à¸à¸à¸¥à¸²à¸ à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸§à¹à¸²à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸´à¸à¸à¸¥à¸²à¸à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸à¸à¸£à¹à¸­à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸°à¸ªà¸²à¸¡à¸²à¸£à¸à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¸°à¹à¸à¹à¸£à¸±à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¹à¹à¸</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">à¹à¸à¸à¸­à¸³à¸à¸²à¸à¸¨à¸²à¸¥à¸à¸²à¸à¹à¸à¸à¹à¸¡à¹à¸­à¸à¸¸à¸à¸²à¸à¹à¸«à¹à¸¡à¸µà¸à¹à¸­à¸¢à¸à¹à¸§à¹à¸à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸³à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸£à¸±à¸à¸à¸£à¸°à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¸£à¸°à¸à¸¸à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸±à¸¢à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸³à¸à¸±à¸à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¸´à¸à¸²à¸¡à¸à¸à¸«à¸¡à¸²à¸¢à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸¹à¹à¸à¸£à¸´à¹à¸ à¸ à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸±à¹à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸¢à¸à¹à¸§à¹à¸à¹à¸¥à¸°à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸³à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¹à¸²à¸à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¸±à¹à¸à¸«à¸¡à¸à¸­à¸²à¸à¸¡à¸´à¹à¸à¹à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸¸à¸</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">7. à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸³à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸£à¸±à¸à¸à¸´à¸</span><b></b></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">à¸à¸£à¸²à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸²à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸à¸«à¸¡à¸²à¸¢à¸à¸µà¹à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸­à¸à¸¸à¸à¸²à¸ Enhance à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¸£à¸´à¸©à¸±à¸à¸£à¹à¸§à¸¡ à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¸¹à¹à¹à¸«à¹à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¸´à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸²à¸à¹à¸¥à¸°à¸à¸¹à¹à¹à¸«à¹à¸à¸£à¸´à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸°à¹à¸¡à¹à¸¡à¸µà¸à¸§à¸²à¸¡à¸£à¸±à¸à¸à¸´à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¹à¸à¸´à¸à¸à¸¶à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¸µà¹à¹à¸à¸µà¹à¸¢à¸§à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¹à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸£à¹à¸à¸§à¸²à¸¡à¸ªà¸²à¸¡à¸²à¸£à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¹à¹à¸à¸¡à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¹à¸à¸·à¹à¸­à¸«à¸²à¹à¸¥à¸°à¸à¸£à¸´à¸à¸²à¸£à¸ªà¸³à¸«à¸£à¸±à¸à¸à¸£à¸à¸µà¸à¸±à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¹à¸à¸à¸µà¹ (à¸) à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸²à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸ à¸à¸§à¸²à¸¡à¹à¸ªà¸µà¸¢à¸«à¸²à¸¢à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸£à¸±à¸à¸¢à¹à¸ªà¸´à¸ à¸à¸¥à¸à¸³à¹à¸£à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸²à¸ à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸­à¸à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¹à¸²à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¸£à¸´à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸à¹à¸à¸ à¸à¸²à¸£à¸ªà¸¹à¸à¹à¸ªà¸µà¸¢à¸à¹à¸­à¸¡à¸¹à¸¥ à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸ªà¸µà¸¢à¹à¸¡à¸à¸£à¸µ à¸à¸²à¸£à¸«à¸¢à¸¸à¸à¸à¸°à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸¸à¸£à¸à¸´à¸ à¸à¸§à¸²à¸¡à¸¥à¹à¸¡à¹à¸«à¸¥à¸§à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸³à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸´à¸à¸à¸¥à¸²à¸à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸­à¸¡à¸à¸´à¸§à¹à¸à¸­à¸£à¹ à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¸¥à¹à¸ªà¸µà¸¢à¸«à¸²à¸¢à¸à¸µà¹à¹à¸à¸´à¸à¸à¸¶à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸ à¸²à¸¢à¸«à¸¥à¸±à¸ à¸à¹à¸²à¹à¸ªà¸µà¸¢à¸«à¸²à¸¢à¸­à¸±à¸à¹à¸à¸·à¹à¸­à¸à¸¡à¸²à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸´à¸à¸ªà¸±à¸à¸à¸² à¸à¸§à¸²à¸¡à¹à¸ªà¸µà¸¢à¸«à¸²à¸¢à¸à¸²à¸à¸­à¹à¸­à¸¡ à¸à¹à¸²à¹à¸ªà¸µà¸¢à¸«à¸²à¸¢à¹à¸à¸´à¸à¸¥à¸à¹à¸à¸© à¸à¸§à¸²à¸¡à¹à¸ªà¸µà¸¢à¸«à¸²à¸¢à¸à¸µà¹à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸° à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¸§à¸²à¸¡à¹à¸ªà¸µà¸¢à¸«à¸²à¸¢à¸à¸µà¹à¸¡à¸µà¸à¸à¸¥à¸à¹à¸à¸© à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­ (à¸) à¸à¹à¸²à¹à¸ªà¸µà¸¢à¸«à¸²à¸¢à¹à¸à¸¢à¸à¸£à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸³à¸à¸§à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¸£à¸§à¸¡à¸à¸±à¸à¹à¸¥à¹à¸§à¹à¸à¸´à¸à¸à¸³à¸à¸§à¸à¹à¸à¸´à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸³à¸£à¸°à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸à¹à¸²à¹à¸à¸¡</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸³à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¹à¸²à¸à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸°à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¹à¸¡à¹à¸§à¹à¸²à¸à¸§à¸²à¸¡à¹à¸ªà¸µà¸¢à¸«à¸²à¸¢à¸à¸µà¹à¹à¸à¸´à¸à¸à¸¶à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸¥à¸°à¹à¸¡à¸´à¸à¸ªà¸±à¸à¸à¸² à¸à¸²à¸£à¸¥à¸°à¹à¸¡à¸´à¸ (à¸£à¸§à¸¡à¸à¸¶à¸à¸à¸§à¸²à¸¡à¸à¸£à¸°à¸¡à¸²à¸à¹à¸¥à¸´à¸à¹à¸¥à¹à¸­) à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¹à¸«à¸à¸¸à¸­à¸·à¹à¸à¹à¸ à¹à¸¥à¸°à¹à¸¡à¹à¸§à¹à¸²à¸à¸§à¸²à¸¡à¹à¸ªà¸µà¸¢à¸«à¸²à¸¢à¸à¸±à¹à¸à¸à¸°à¸ªà¸²à¸¡à¸²à¸£à¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¹à¹à¸à¹à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¹à¸¡à¹ à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­ Enhance à¸à¸°à¹à¸à¹à¸£à¸±à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¸·à¸­à¸à¸à¸¶à¸à¸à¸§à¸²à¸¡à¹à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸°à¹à¸à¸´à¸à¸à¸§à¸²à¸¡à¹à¸ªà¸µà¸¢à¸«à¸²à¸¢à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸¥à¹à¸²à¸§&nbsp; à¸à¸²à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸­à¸³à¸à¸²à¸à¸¨à¸²à¸¥à¹à¸¡à¹à¸­à¸à¸¸à¸à¸²à¸à¹à¸«à¹à¸¡à¸µà¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸³à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸§à¸²à¸¡à¸£à¸±à¸à¸à¸´à¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸£à¸°à¸à¸²à¸£ à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸±à¹à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸³à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸§à¸²à¸¡à¸£à¸±à¸à¸à¸´à¸à¸à¹à¸²à¸à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸£à¸°à¸à¸²à¸£à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¸±à¹à¸à¸«à¸¡à¸à¸­à¸²à¸à¹à¸¡à¹à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸¸à¸</span></p>
<p><b>8. à¸à¸²à¸£à¸£à¸°à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸´à¸à¸²à¸à¹à¸à¸¢à¸à¸²à¸£à¸­à¸à¸¸à¸à¸²à¹à¸à¸à¸¸à¸¥à¸²à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸µà¹à¸¡à¸µà¸à¸¥à¸à¸¹à¸à¸à¸±à¸ (à¹à¸à¸£à¸à¸­à¹à¸²à¸à¸«à¸¡à¸§à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¸­à¸¢à¹à¸²à¸à¸¥à¸°à¹à¸­à¸µà¸¢à¸à¹à¸à¸·à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸°à¸¡à¸µà¸à¸¥à¸à¹à¸­à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¸´à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸¸à¸)</b></p>
<ul>
<li><span style="font-weight: 400;">8.1 à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸±à¸à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸²à¸</span><span style="font-weight: 400;">&nbsp; à¸«à¸¡à¸§à¸à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸£à¸°à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸´à¸à¸²à¸à¹à¸à¸¢à¸à¸²à¸£à¸­à¸à¸¸à¸à¸²à¹à¸à¸à¸¸à¸¥à¸²à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸µà¹à¸¡à¸µà¸à¸¥à¸à¸¹à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¹à¸£à¸µà¸¢à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸ âà¸ªà¸±à¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸²à¸£à¸­à¸à¸¸à¸à¸²à¹à¸à¸à¸¸à¸¥à¸²à¸à¸²à¸£â à¹à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¸à¸à¸µà¹&nbsp; à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸à¸¥à¸à¸§à¹à¸²à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸´à¸à¸²à¸à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¹à¸­à¹à¸£à¸µà¸¢à¸à¸£à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸±à¹à¸à¸«à¸¡à¸à¹à¸ à¹ à¸à¸µà¹à¹à¸à¹à¹à¸à¸´à¸à¸à¸¶à¹à¸à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸­à¸²à¸à¹à¸à¸´à¸à¸à¸¶à¹à¸à¸£à¸°à¸«à¸§à¹à¸²à¸à¸à¸¸à¸à¹à¸¥à¸° Enhance à¹à¸¡à¹à¸§à¹à¸²à¹à¸à¸´à¸à¸à¸¶à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¹à¸à¸¢à¹à¸à¸µà¹à¸¢à¸§à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¸à¸à¸µà¹ (à¸£à¸§à¸¡à¸à¸¶à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸¥à¹à¸²à¸§à¸«à¸²à¸à¸¶à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸¥à¸°à¹à¸¡à¸´à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¸) à¸à¸£à¸´à¸à¸²à¸£ à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¸©à¸à¸²à¹à¸ à¹ à¹à¸à¹à¸¡à¸¸à¸¡à¹à¸ à¹ à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸§à¸²à¸¡à¸ªà¸±à¸¡à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¹à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¸¸à¸£à¸à¸£à¸£à¸¡à¸£à¸°à¸«à¸§à¹à¸²à¸à¹à¸£à¸² à¸à¸°à¸à¸³à¸à¸²à¸£à¸£à¸°à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¹à¸²à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸­à¸à¸¸à¸à¸²à¹à¸à¸à¸¸à¸¥à¸²à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸µà¹à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¸ªà¸¸à¸à¹à¸¥à¸°à¸¡à¸µà¸à¸¥à¸à¸¹à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸²à¸à¸±à¹à¸ à¸¡à¸²à¸à¹à¸ªà¸µà¸¢à¸à¸§à¹à¸²à¸à¸°à¸à¸³à¹à¸à¸´à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸µà¹à¸¨à¸²à¸¥ à¸à¸²à¸¡à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸³à¸«à¸à¸à¸à¸­à¸à¸ªà¸±à¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸²à¸£à¸­à¸à¸¸à¸à¸²à¹à¸à¸à¸¸à¸¥à¸²à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸µà¹ à¸¢à¸à¹à¸§à¹à¸à¸§à¹à¸²à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸°à¸à¸³à¸à¹à¸­à¹à¸£à¸µà¸¢à¸à¸£à¹à¸­à¸à¸ªà¹à¸§à¸à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸¥à¹à¸à¸¨à¸²à¸¥à¸à¸à¸µà¸¡à¹à¸à¸ªà¸²à¹à¸£à¹ à¸«à¸²à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¹à¸£à¸µà¸¢à¸à¸£à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸¸à¸à¸¡à¸µà¸à¸¸à¸à¸ªà¸¡à¸à¸±à¸à¸´à¹à¸à¸µà¸¢à¸à¸à¸­&nbsp; à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸µà¹ à¸ªà¸±à¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸²à¸£à¸­à¸à¸¸à¸à¸²à¹à¸à¸à¸¸à¸¥à¸²à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸µà¹à¹à¸¡à¹à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸±à¸à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¸´à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸¸à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸¢à¸à¸à¸£à¸°à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸ªà¸¹à¹à¸«à¸à¹à¸§à¸¢à¸à¸²à¸à¸ªà¸«à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸£à¸±à¸ à¸«à¸à¹à¸§à¸¢à¸à¸²à¸à¸£à¸±à¸ à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸«à¸à¹à¸§à¸¢à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸´à¹à¸ à¹à¸¥à¸°à¸«à¸à¹à¸§à¸¢à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸¥à¹à¸²à¸§à¸ªà¸²à¸¡à¸²à¸£à¸à¹à¸ªà¸§à¸à¸«à¸²à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸¢à¸µà¸¢à¸§à¸¢à¸²à¸à¹à¸­à¹à¸£à¸²à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸¡à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸¸à¸à¹à¸à¹ à¸«à¸²à¸à¸à¸à¸«à¸¡à¸²à¸¢à¸­à¸à¸¸à¸à¸²à¸&nbsp; à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸à¸¥à¸à¸§à¹à¸² à¹à¸à¸¢à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¹à¸²à¸à¸³à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¸à¸à¸µà¹ à¸à¸¸à¸à¹à¸¥à¸° Enhance à¸à¹à¸²à¸à¸ªà¸¥à¸°à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¸´à¹à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸´à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸¢à¸¥à¸¹à¸à¸à¸¸à¸à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¹à¸à¹à¸²à¸£à¹à¸§à¸¡à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸¡à¸à¸¥à¸¸à¹à¸¡à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸¥&nbsp; à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¸´à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸°à¹à¸à¹à¸£à¸±à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸±à¸à¸ªà¸´à¸à¹à¸à¸¢à¸­à¸à¸¸à¸à¸²à¹à¸à¸à¸¸à¸¥à¸²à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸µà¹à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸¥à¸²à¸ à¸¡à¸´à¹à¸à¹à¹à¸à¸¢à¸à¸¹à¹à¸à¸´à¸à¸²à¸à¸©à¸²à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¸à¸°à¸¥à¸¹à¸à¸à¸¸à¸&nbsp; à¸à¸£à¸°à¸£à¸²à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸´à¸­à¸à¸¸à¸à¸²à¹à¸à¸à¸¸à¸¥à¸²à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸«à¹à¸à¸ªà¸«à¸£à¸±à¸à¸à¸°à¹à¸à¹à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸µà¸à¸§à¸²à¸¡à¹à¸¥à¸°à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸ªà¸±à¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸²à¸£à¸­à¸à¸¸à¸à¸²à¹à¸à¸à¸¸à¸¥à¸²à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸µà¹</span></li>
<li>8.2 à¸à¹à¸­à¸«à¹à¸²à¸¡à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸¡à¸à¸¥à¸¸à¹à¸¡à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸¥à¹à¸¥à¸°à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸¢à¸à¸¹à¹à¹à¸à¸à¹à¸¥à¸°à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸¢à¸µà¸¢à¸§à¸¢à¸²à¸à¸µà¹à¹à¸¡à¹à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸£à¸²à¸¢à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸¥<br>
<i>à¸à¸¸à¸à¹à¸¥à¸° </i><b><i>Enhance</i></b><i> à¸à¸à¸¥à¸à¸§à¹à¸²à¹à¸à¹à¸¥à¸°à¸à¹à¸²à¸¢à¸à¸°à¸ªà¸²à¸¡à¸²à¸£à¸à¹à¸£à¸µà¸¢à¸à¸£à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸­à¸µà¸à¸à¹à¸²à¸¢à¹à¸à¹à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸£à¸²à¸¢à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸¥à¹à¸à¹à¸²à¸à¸±à¹à¸à¹à¸¥à¸°à¹à¸¡à¹à¹à¸à¹à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸°à¹à¸à¸à¸à¹à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸ªà¸¡à¸²à¸à¸´à¸à¸à¸¥à¸¸à¹à¸¡à¹à¸à¸à¸¥à¸¸à¹à¸¡à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸¡à¸à¸¥à¸¸à¹à¸¡à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸¥à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¹à¸à¸¢à¸à¸¹à¹à¹à¸à¸à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸³à¹à¸à¸´à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸ à¹&nbsp; à¹à¸§à¹à¸à¹à¸ªà¸µà¸¢à¹à¸à¹à¸§à¹à¸²à¸à¸±à¹à¸à¸à¸¸à¸à¹à¸¥à¸° </i><b><i>Enhance</i></b><i> à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸¥à¸à¹à¸§à¹à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸­à¸·à¹à¸ à¸­à¸à¸¸à¸à¸²à¹à¸à¸à¸¸à¸¥à¸²à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸¡à¹à¸­à¸²à¸à¸£à¸§à¸¡à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¹à¸à¹à¸²à¸£à¹à¸§à¸¡à¸à¹à¸­à¹à¸£à¸µà¸¢à¸à¸£à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸¥à¸¡à¸²à¸à¸à¸§à¹à¸²à¸«à¸à¸¶à¹à¸à¸à¸à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸«à¸à¸¶à¹à¸à¸à¹à¸²à¸¢à¹à¸¥à¸°à¹à¸¡à¹à¸­à¸²à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸£à¸°à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸´à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸à¸£à¸§à¸¡ à¹à¸à¸¢à¸à¸¹à¹à¹à¸à¸ à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸¡à¸à¸¥à¸¸à¹à¸¡à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸¥à¹à¸¡à¹à¸§à¹à¸²à¹à¸à¸£à¸¹à¸à¹à¸à¸à¹à¸&nbsp; <li>8.8 à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¸¥à¸µà¹à¸¢à¸à¹à¸à¸¥à¸à¸ªà¸±à¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸²à¸£à¸­à¸à¸¸à¸à¸²à¹à¸à¸à¸¸à¸¥à¸²à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¸­à¸à¸²à¸à¸&nbsp; à¹à¸¡à¹à¸§à¹à¸²à¸à¹à¸­à¸ªà¸±à¸à¸à¸²à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸°à¸¡à¸µà¸à¸§à¸²à¸¡à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸±à¸à¹à¸¢à¹à¸ Enhance à¸à¸à¸¥à¸à¸§à¹à¸²à¸«à¸²à¸à¸à¸£à¸´à¸©à¸±à¸à¹à¸à¸¥à¸µà¹à¸¢à¸à¹à¸à¸¥à¸à¸ªà¸±à¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸²à¸£à¸­à¸à¸¸à¸à¸²à¹à¸à¸à¸¸à¸¥à¸²à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸µà¹à¹à¸à¹à¸­à¸¢à¹à¸²à¸à¹à¸ (à¸à¸­à¸à¹à¸«à¸à¸·à¸­à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¸¥à¸µà¹à¸¢à¸à¹à¸à¸¥à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¸­à¸¢à¸¹à¹à¸ªà¸³à¸«à¸£à¸±à¸à¸ªà¹à¸à¸à¸³à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¹à¸²à¸§) à¸à¸à¸°à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸¸à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸à¸¹à¹à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸£à¸´à¸à¸²à¸£ à¸à¸¸à¸à¸ªà¸²à¸¡à¸²à¸£à¸à¸à¸à¸´à¹à¸ªà¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¸¥à¸µà¹à¸¢à¸à¹à¸à¸¥à¸à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸¥à¹à¸²à¸§à¹à¸à¹à¹à¸à¸¢à¸ªà¹à¸à¸à¸³à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¹à¸²à¸§à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸¥à¸²à¸¢à¸¥à¸±à¸à¸©à¸à¹à¸­à¸±à¸à¸©à¸£à¸¡à¸²à¸¢à¸±à¸ Enhance à¸ à¸²à¸¢à¹à¸à¸ªà¸²à¸¡à¸ªà¸´à¸ (30) à¸§à¸±à¸à¸à¸²à¸¡à¸à¸à¸´à¸à¸´à¸à¹à¸£à¸·à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¸¥à¸µà¹à¸¢à¸à¹à¸à¸¥à¸à¸¡à¸²à¸¢à¸±à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¸­à¸¢à¸¹à¹à¸ªà¸³à¸«à¸£à¸±à¸à¸ªà¹à¸à¸à¸³à¸à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¹à¸²à¸§à¸à¹à¸²à¸à¸à¹à¸&nbsp; à¹à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸à¸´à¹à¸ªà¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¸¥à¸µà¹à¸¢à¸à¹à¸à¸¥à¸à¹à¸à¸­à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¹à¸ à¹ à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸à¸¥à¸à¹à¸à¸¢à¸à¸£à¸´à¸¢à¸²à¸¢à¸à¸§à¹à¸²à¸à¸¸à¸à¸à¸°à¸à¸³à¹à¸à¸´à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸±à¸à¸ªà¸´à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸²à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸´à¸à¸²à¸à¹à¸ à¹ à¸£à¸°à¸«à¸§à¹à¸²à¸à¹à¸£à¸²à¸à¸²à¸¡à¸ à¸²à¸©à¸²à¸à¸­à¸à¸ªà¸±à¸à¸à¸²à¸à¸²à¸£à¸­à¸à¸¸à¸à¸²à¹à¸à¸à¸¸à¸¥à¸²à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸±à¸à¸à¸±à¹à¸à¹à¸à¹à¸§à¸±à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸µà¹à¸à¸¸à¸à¸¢à¸­à¸¡à¸£à¸±à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¸à¸à¸µà¹à¹à¸à¹à¸à¸§à¸±à¸à¹à¸£à¸ (à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­à¸¢à¸­à¸¡à¸£à¸±à¸à¸à¸²à¸£à¹à¸à¸¥à¸µà¹à¸¢à¸à¹à¸à¸¥à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸à¸à¸¥à¸à¸à¹à¸­à¸¡à¸²à¹à¸ à¹)</li>
